## Diagram 3

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class Hold {
        +number id
        +string activatedComments
        +string activatedEventDate
        +string activatedReceiveDate
        +string clearedComments
        +string clearedEventDate
        +string clearedReceiveDate
        +string status
        +string type
        +string typeName
        +string type_name
    }
    
    class Exception {
        +number id
        +string activatedComments
        +string activatedEventDate
        +string activatedReceiveDate
        +string clearedComments
        +string clearedEventDate
        +string clearedReceiveDate
        +string severity
        +string status
        +string type
        +string name
        +string typeName
    }
    
    class ExceptionsBoxProps {
        +Hold[] holds
        +boolean showAllException
        +Exception[] exceptions
        +boolean shouldBuildExceptionsBySeverity
        +boolean showExpectedClearDate
        +string expectedClearDate
        +string customExceptionBoxColor
        +CSSProperties style
    }
    
    ExceptionsBoxProps --> Hold
    ExceptionsBoxProps --> Exception
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> ProcessExceptions
    ProcessExceptions --> CalculateCounts: Build exception counts
    CalculateCounts --> DetermineColor: Sum totals
    DetermineColor --> CustomColor: Has custom color
    DetermineColor --> StandardColor: No custom color
    CustomColor --> RenderBox
    StandardColor --> RenderBox
    RenderBox --> ShowList: Has exceptions
    RenderBox --> ShowEmpty: No exceptions
    ShowList --> CheckClearDate
    ShowEmpty --> CheckClearDate
    CheckClearDate --> ShowDate: Date exists
    CheckClearDate --> [*]: No date
    ShowDate --> [*]
```
